# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
S' abacate tam n;

S  abacaxi tam m;

custo troca = 10;
remoção = 7;
insere = 6;

f(int n, int m){
if(n==0)return 6*m
if(m==0)return 7*n
if(JC[n][m])return memo[n][m]
int ctr= 10+f(n-1,m-1);
int cre= 7+f(n-1,m);
int cin= 6+f(n,m-1);
return min(ctr,cre,cin);
} ^m8tPAcvg

Frostfree ^HKGHVhfD
